posted:Posted May 14, 2024
msg:There are not many choices of hotels in Shantou. Hotels in the city are very convenient, but they are generally old. This hotel opened in 2013. Although it is a little remote in Longhu District, it is relatively quiet. The surrounding area is also relatively deserted, and there is no place suitable for walking. There is a trail downstairs, but there is no scenery to speak of. The lobby is on the 27th floor, and the guest rooms are on the 28th to 38th floors. There are sufficient underground garages, but you have to take 3 elevators from the garage to the room, which is a bit troublesome. The room hardware is new, and the hygiene is good as long as you don't look at it with a magnifying glass. It is a relatively standard modern and simple design. Some details are also well done, such as the clothesline in the shower room, and the curtains have a very good blackout effect, but the room soundproofing is average. The service is basically polite and good. It is a good choice in Shantou.

In this way, people at each level of the elevator will be diverted, which is a good design.
